Ran out of threads.\n");\n  23                 last;\n  24             }\n  25         }\n  26     }\n  27     if ($kid) {\n  28         $downstream->enqueue(undef);\n  29         $kid->join();\n  30     }\n  31 }\n  32\n  33 my $stream = Thread::Queue->new(3..1000, undef);\n  34 check_num($stream, 2);\n')
